5a3('bum): gyis gnas pa'i snyems par 'jug pa dgu med pa dang / rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa med pa dang / mngon par shes pa rnams med
5a4('bum): pa dang / ting nge 'dzin rnams med pa dang / gzungs kyi sgo rnams med pa dang / gang la de bzhin gshegs pa'i stob sa rnams med pa dang / mi 'jigs pa rnams med pa dang /

5a7('bum): cad shes pa nyid med pa dang / lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid med pa dang / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub med pa de ni rang bzhin stong pa nyid de/ de la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa'
5a8('bum): sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod de/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod cing / sems can phyin ci log tu gyur pa rnams sems can gyi 'du shes las 'grel te/ 
5b1('bum): gzugs kyi 'du shes las 'grel to// gzugs med pa'i 'du shes las 'grel to// zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos thams cad kyi bar las 'grel to// zag pa med pa'i chos 'di lta ste/ dran
5b2('bum): panye bar gzhag pa bzhi dang / yang dag par spong ba bzhi dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi dang / dbang po lnga dang / stobs lnga dang / byang chub kyi yang lag bdun dang / 'phags pa'i lam yang lag brgyad pa dang / 
5b3('bum): rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum dang / 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi dang / rnam par thar pa brgyad dang / mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu dang / ting nge 'dzin thams cad dang / gzugs kyi sku
5b4('bum): cad dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / mi 'ji gas pa bzhi dang / so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi dang / byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi
5b5('bum): ma 'dres pa bco brgyad po de dag kyang de la don dam pa'i rnam pa gang yin pa de lta bu ma yin te/ 'di ltar 'dus ma byas ba dang / ma skyes pa dang / dngos po med pa dang / 'byung ba med pa

7a6('bum): gyis mi stong pa ma yid de// de bas na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod cing / sems cad du 'du shes pa'i sems can rnams

7b1('bum): byas/ sems can rnams yongs su smin par byas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongasu dag par byas nas/ tshe'i 'du byed byin gyis brlabs te/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang

10a6('bum): kyang gzhan no// 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams kyang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// bsam gtan rnams kyang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhano// /

10a8('bum): rnam par thar pa brgyad kyang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu yang gzhan no// rang bzhin steng pa nyid kyang
10b1('bum): gzhan no// rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa nyid kyang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// mngon par shes pa rnams
10b2('bum): kyang gzhan no// rang bzhin steng ba nyid kyang gzhan no// ting nge 'dzin rnams kyang gzhano// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// gzungs kyi sgo rnams kyang gzhan no// rang
10b3('bum): bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ne// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu yang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// mi 'jigs pa bzhi yang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong
10b4('bum): pa nyid kyang gzhan de// se so yang dag par rig pa bzhi yang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// byams pa chen po yang gzhan no// rang bzhin steng ba
10b5('bum): nyid kyang gzhan no// snying rje chen po yang gzhan ne// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// sangs rgyas kyi cha sa ma 'dres pa bco brgyad kyang gzhan no// rang bzhin
10b6('bum): stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu yang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu yang gzhan ne// rang bzhin stong
10b7('bum): pa nyid kyang gzhan no// phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu yang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// dgra bcom pa nyid kyang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan ne// 
10b8('bum): rang byang chub kyang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid kyang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan no// rnam pa thams cad
11a1('bum): mkhyen pa nyid kyang gzhan no// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzhan do// zhes bgyi bar rang bzhin steng pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi bgyid kyi/ gzugs
11a2('bum): nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzugs so// tshor ba nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid kyang tshor ba'o// 'du shes nyid kyang rang
11a3('bum): bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang 'du shes so// 'du byed nyid kyang rang bzhin steng pa nyid de// rang bzhin steng pa nyid kyang 'du byed do// rnam par shes pa nyid kyang
11a4('bum): rang bzhin steng pa nyid de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang rnam par shes pa'o// mig nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid kyang mig go/ rna ba nyid kyang
11a5('bum): rang bzhin stong pa nyid de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang rna ba sna nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin steng ba nyid kyang sna'o// lce nyid kyang rang bzhin steng pa nyid de// 
11a6('bum): rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang lce'o// lus nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang lus so// yid nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang yid de/ 
11a7('bum): gzugs nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang gzugs so// sgra nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang sgra'o// dri nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid
11a8('bum): rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang dri'o// ro nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang ro'o// reg nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid kyang reg go/ 
11b1('bum): chos nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang chos so// mig gi rnam par shes pa nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang mig gi rnam par
11b2('bum): shes pa'o// rna ba'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'o// sna'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// 
11b3('bum): rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang sna'i rnam par shes pa'o// lce'i rnam par shes pa nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang lce'i rnam par shes pa'o// lus kyi rnam
11b4('bum): bar shes pa nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhi na stong pa nyid kyang lus kyi rnam par shes pa'o// yid kyi rnam par shes pa nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do//

11b8('bum): kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'o// yid kyi 'dus te reg pa nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang yid
12a1('bum): kyi 'dus te reg pa'o// mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i

12a6('bum): pa nyid kyang yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'o// sa'i khams kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang sa'i khams so// chu'i khams nyid kyang rang bzhin steng
12a7('bum): ba nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang chu'i khams so// me'i khams nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang me'i khams so// rlung gi khams nyid kyang rang bzhin
12a8('bum): stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang rlung gi khams so// na mkha'i khams nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang na mkha'i khams so// rnam par
12b1('bum): shes pa'i khams nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhid stong pa nyid kyang rnam par shes pa'i khams so// ma rig pa nyid kyang rang bzhin stong pa nyid do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyang

41b7('bum): rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni 'du byed do// 'di ni 'du byed kyi stong pa nyid de zhes 'du byed rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rnam par shes

42a1('bum): zhes mig rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rna ba'o// 'di ni rna ba'i steng pa nyid de zhes rnab rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de/ 
42a2('bum): rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni sna'o// 'di ni sna'i steng pa nyid de zhes sna rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni lce'o// 'di ri lce'i stong pa nyid do zhes
42a3('bum): rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni lus so// 'di ni lus kyi stong pa nyid do zhes lus rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni
42a4('bum): 'di ni yid de// 'di ni yid kyi stong pa nyid do zhes yid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin steng ba nyid ni 'di ni gzugaso// 'di ni gzugs kyi steng ba
42a5('bum): nyid do zhes gzugs rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni sgra'o// 'di ni sgra 'i stong pa nyid do zhes sgra rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// 
42a6('bum): rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni dri'o// 'di ni dri'i stong pa nyid do zhes dri rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni ro'o// 'di ni ro'i stong pa nyid do/ 
42a7('bum): zhes ro rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni reg go/ 'di ni reg gi stong pa nyid do zhes reg rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhir stong pa
42a8('bum): nyid ni 'di ni ches so// 'di ni chos kyi stong pa nyid do zhes chos rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni mig gi rnam par shes pa'o// 'di ni
42b1('bum): mig gi rnam par shes pa'i steng pa nyid do zhes mig gi rnam par shes pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'o// 'di ni rna ba'i rnam
42b2('bum): par shes pa'i steng pa nyid do zhes rna ba'i rnam par shes pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid ni 'di ni sna'i rnam par shes pa'o// 'di ni sna'i rnam par shes
42b3('bum): pa'i steng pa nyid do zhes sna'i rnam par shes pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid ni 'di ni lce'i rnam par shes pa'o// 'di ni lce'i rnam par shes pa'i
42b4('bum): steng pa nyid de zhes lce'i rnam par shes pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhin steng pa nyid ni 'dini lus kyi rnam par shes pa'o// 'di ni lus kyi rnam
42b5('bum): par shes pa'i steng pa nyid de zhes lus kyi rnam par shes pa rnam par la drug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa'o// 
42b6('bum): 'di ni yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes yid kyi rnam par shes pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni mig gi 'dus te reg pa'o// 'di
42b7('bum): ni mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes mig gi 'dus te reg pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid ni 'di ni rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'o// 'di ni/ 
42b8('bum): ba'i 'dus te rig pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa rnam par 'a khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni sna'i 'dus te reg pa'o// 'di ni snga'i 'dus
43a1('bum): te reg pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes snga'i 'dus te reg pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhid stong pa 'di ni 'di ni lce'i 'dus te reg pa'o// 'ja
43a2('bum): ni lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes lce'i 'dus te reg pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid de 'di ni lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'o// 'di ni lus
43a3('bum): kyi 'dus te reg pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes lus kyi 'dus te reg pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'o// 'dir
43a4('bum): yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes yid kyi 'dus te reg pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni mig gi 'dus te reg pa las byung
43a5('bum): ba'i tsher ba'o// 'di ni mig gi 'dus te reg pa la sa byung ba'i tsher ba'i steng pa nyid do zhes mig gi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba rnam par 'khrug par
43a6('bum): mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'o// 'di ni rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tsher ba'i stong pa nyid do zhes rna ba'i
43a7('bum): 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni sna'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tsher ba'o// 'di ni sna'i 'dus te
43a8('bum): reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'i stong pa nyid do zhes sna'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid ni 'di ni lce'i 'dus te reg
43b1('bum): pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'o// 'di ni lce'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'i stong pa nyid do zhes lce'i 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// 
43b2('bum): rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni lus kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'o// 'di ni lus kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'i stong pa nyid do zhes lus kyi 'dus te reg pa las
43b3('bum): byung ba'i tshor ba rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni yid kyi 'dus te reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba'o// 'di ni yid kyi 'dus te rig pa las byung
43b4('bum): ba'i tshor ba'i stong pa nyid do zhes yid kyi 'dus te reg pa lngas byung ba'i tshor ba rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni sa'i khamaso// 'di ni
43b5('bum): sa'i khams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes sa'i khams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni chu'i khams so// 'di ni chu'i khams kyi stong pa
43b6('bum): nyid do zhes chu'i khams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni me'i khams so// 'di ni me'i khams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes me'i khams rnam par 'khrug par
43b7('bum): mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rlung gi khams so// 'di ni rlung gi khams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes rlung gi khams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni
43b8('bum): 'di ni namakha'i khams so// 'di ni na mkha'i khams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes na mkha'i khams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rnam par shes pa'i
44a1('bum): khams so// 'di ni rnam par shes pa'i khams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes rnam par shes pa'i khams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni
44a2('bum): 'di ni ma rig pa'o// 'di ni ma rig pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes ma rig pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni 'du byed do// 'di ni 'du byed kyi stong pa nyid
44a3('bum): do zhes 'du byed rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rnam par shes pa'o// 'di ni rnam par shes pa'i steng pa nyid do zhes rnam par shes pa rnam par
44a4('bum): 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid ni 'di ni ming dang gzugs so// 'di ni ming dang gzugs kyi stong pa nyid do zhes ming dang gzugs rnam par 'khrug par mi byed
44a5('bum): dorang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni skye mched drug go/ 'di ni skye mched drug gi stong pa nyid do zhes skye mched drug rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa
44a6('bum): nyid ni 'di ni reg pa'o// 'di ni reg pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes reg pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni tshor ba'o// 'di ni tsher ba'i stong pa nyid de zhes
44a7('bum): tsher ba rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni sred pa'o// 'di ni sred pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes sred pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong
44a8('bum): pa nyid ni 'di ni len pa'o// 'di ni len pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes len pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni srid pa'o// 'di ni srid pa'i stong pa nyid do/ 
44b1('bum): zhes srid pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid ni 'di ni skye ba'o// 'di ni skye ba'i steng pa nyid do zhes skye ba rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa
44b2('bum): nyid ni 'di ni rga shi'o// 'di ni rga shi'i stong pa nyid de zhes rga shi rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa 'di ni 'di ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'dir spyod pa'i
44b3('bum): pha rol tu phyin pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes sbrid pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni
44b4('bum): tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni bzod
44b5('bum): pa'i pha rol tu phyid pa'o// 'di de bzong ba'i ba rol tu phyin pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes bzed pa'i pa rol tu phyin pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// 
44b6('bum): rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i stong pa nyid do// zhes brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam
44b7('bum): bar 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid de/ 'di ni bsapa gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyir ba'i stong pa nyid do zhes
44b8('bum): bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid ni/ 'di ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni shes rab kyi
45a1('bum): pha rol tu phyin pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhi stong pa 'di ni/ 'di ni dang
45a2('bum): stong pa nyid do// 'di ni nang stong pa nyid kyi stong pa nyid do zhes nang stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni phyi steng pa nyid do// 'di
45a3('bum): phyi stong pa nyid kyi stong pa nyid do zhes phyi stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni phyi nang stong pa nyid do// 'di ni phyi dang stong pa nyid kyi stong pa
45a4('bum): nyid do zhes phyi rang stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni stong pa nyid stong pa nyid do// 'di ni stong pa nyid stong pa nyid kyi steng pa
45a5('bum): nyid do zhes stong pa nyid stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni chen bo stong pa nyid do// 'di ni chen po stong pa nyid kyi
45a6('bum): stong pa nyid do zhes chen po stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni don dam pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni der dam pa stong pa nyid kyi stong pa
45a7('bum): nyid do zhes don dam pa stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni 'dus byas stong pa nyid do// 'di ni 'dus byas stong pa nyid kyi stong pa nyid do/ 
45a8('bum): zhes 'dus byas stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid do// 'di ni 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid kyi stong pa nyid de
45b1('bum): zhes 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni mtha' las 'das pa steng pa nyid
45b2('bum): kyi stong pa nyid do zhes mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni thog pa dang thal
45b3('bum): med pa stong pa nyid kyi stong pa nyid do zhes theg sa ngas lalang stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni dor ba med pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni dor ba med pa stong pa nyid kyi
45b4('bum): stong pa nyid do zhes der ba med pa stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rang ba zhin stong pa nyid do// 'di ni rang bzhin stong pa nyid kyi stong
45b5('bum): pa nyid do zhes rang bzhin stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni chos thams cang stong pa nyid do// 'di ni chos thams cad stong pa nyid kyi
45b6('bum): stong pa nyid do zhes chos thams cad stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid do// 'di ni rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid kyi stong pa
45b7('bum): nyid de zhes rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin steng pa nyid ni 'di ni mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid kyi stong pa nyid do/ 
45b8('bum): zhes mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni dngos po med pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni dngos po med pa stong pa nyid kyi stong pa nyid do zhes dngos po
46a1('bum): med pa stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do// 'di ni ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyi stong pa nyid do zhes ngo bo nyid
46a2('bum): stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do// 'di ni dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid kyi stong pa nyid do zhes dngos po
46a3('bum): med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams so// 'di ni dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams kyi stong
46a4('bum): pa nyid do zhes ngan pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams rnam par 'khrug bar mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni yang dag par spong ba rnams so// 'di ni yang dag par spong
46a5('bum): ba rnams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes yang dag par spong ba rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// ra bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams
46a6('bum): so/ 'di ni rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni dbang po
46a7('bum): rnams so// 'di ni dbang po rnams kyi stong pa'ing ngo zhes dbang po rnams rnam par 'a khrug par mi byed // rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni skabs rnams pa// 'don sngas
46a8('bum): rnams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes stobs rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni byang chub kyi yan lag rnams sa// 'di di byang chub kyi yan lag rnams kyi
46b1('bum): stong pa nyid do zhes byang chub kyi yan lag rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa'o// 'di ni 'phags pa'i
46b2('bum): lam yan lag brgyad pa'i steng pa nyid de zhes 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams so// 
46b3('bum): 'di ni 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni bsam gtan rnams
46b4('bum): se 'di ri bsam gtan rnams kyi stong pa nyid do/ zhes bsam gtan rnams rnam par 'khrug pa ra mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag
46b5('bum): ni tshad med pa rnams so// 'di ni tshad med pa rnam sa kyi stong pa nyid de zhes tshad med pa rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag
46b6('bum): ni gzugs med pa'i snyems par 'jug pa rnams so// 'di ni gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes gzugs meng pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams rnam par
46b7('bum): 'khrug par mi byed de// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni rnam par thar pa rnams so// 'di ni rnam par thar pa rnams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes rnam par thar pa rnams rnam par 'khrug
46b8('bum): par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams so// 'di ni mthar gyis gnas pa'i sems par 'jug pa rnams kyi sring pa
47a1('bum): nyid do zhes mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ri steng pa nyid dang
47a2('bum): mtshan pa med pa dang / smod pa med pa'o// 'di ni stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'i stong pa nyid do zhes stong pa nyid dang / mdzan pa med pa dang / smon pa med pa
47a3('bum): rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni mngon par shes pa rnams so// 'di ni mngon par shes pa rnams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes mngon par shes pa
47a4('bum): rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang ba zhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni ting nge 'dzin rnams so// 'di ni ting nge 'dzin rnams kyi steng pa nying ngo zhes
47a5('bum): ting nge 'dzin rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni gzungs kyi sgo rnam sa so// 'di ni gzungs kyi sgra rnams kyi stong pa nyid
47a6('bum): do zhes gzungs kyi sgo rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu'o// 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs
47a7('bum): bcu'i stong pa nyid de zhes de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni mi 'jigs pa rnams so// 'di ni mi 'jigs pa rnams
47a8('bum): kyi stong pa nyid do zhes mi 'jigs pa rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag na so so yang dag par rig pa rnams// 'din so so yang dag par rig pa rnams
47b1('bum): kyi stong pa nyid do zhes so so yang dag par rig pa rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni byams pa chen po'o// 'di ni byams pa chen po'i stong pa nyid do
47b2('bum): zhes byams pa chen po rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di dag ni snying rje chen po'o// 'di ni snying rje chen po'i stong pa nyid do zhes snying rje chen po rnam par 'khru
47b3('bum): par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'od dag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams so// 'di dag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams kyi stong pa nyid do zhes sangs rgyas kyi
47b4('bum): chos ma 'dres pa rnams rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di na rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'o// 'di ni rgyur du zhugs pa'i 'bras
47b5('bum): bu'i stong pa nyid do zhes rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o// 
47b6('bum): 'di ni lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'i stong pa nyid do zhes lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o// 
47b7('bum): 'di ni phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu stong pa nyid do zhes phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni dgra bcom pa nyid do// 'di ni dgra ba
47b8('bum): ba nyid kyi stong pa nyid do zhes dgra bcom pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di ni rang byang chub bo// 'di ni rang byang chub kyi steng pa nyid do zhes rang byang chub
48a1('bum): rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni 'di na byang chubabo// 'di ni byang chub kyi stong pa nyid de zhes byang chub rnam par 'khrug par
48a2('bum): byed do// / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa steng phrag brgya pa/ be rab 'byor 'di lta ste/ dper na/ 
48a3('bum): namakha' ni nam mkha' rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// nang gi nam mkha' ni phyi'i namakha' rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// phyi'i namakha' ni nang gi nimakha' rnam par 'khrug par
48a4('bum): mi byed do// rab 'byor de bzhin du gzugs kyang stong pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// stong pa nyid kyang gzugs rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// tshor ba 'ang
48a5('bum): steng pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed/ stong pa nyid kyang tshor ba rnam par 'khrug par mi byed do// 'du shes kya nga steng pa nyid rnam par 'khrug par mi byed/ stong pa nyid

54b4('bum): pa nyid de// 'di dag ri dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams/ 'dir steng pa nyid de// 'di dag ni yang dag par spong ba rnams/ 'dir stong pa nyid do// 'di dag ri rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams/

55a1('bum): pa med pa dang / sped pa med pa 'di ri stong pa nyid de// 'di dag ni mngon par shes pa rnams/ 'dir stong pa nyid de// 'di dag ni ting nge 'dzin rnams/ 'di ri stong pa nyid de//

55b1('bum): tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar mi nus so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de de bzhin re// de de bzhin te/ byang chub gnyis su dper med pa ste/ gnyis la skyed pa la

55b3('bum): gnyis su bya ba la mi sbed do// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang rkub de ni/ gzugs la mi spyod de// tshor ba la mi spyod de// 'du shes la mi skyed de// 'du byed la mi skyed de/

56a1('bum): spyod do// lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la mi skyed do// yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyer gyis tshor ba la pi skyed do// sa'i khams la mi skyed de// du'i khams la mi

56b1('bum): la mi sbed de// ngo bo nyid steng pa nyid la mi skyed do// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la mi skyed de// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams la mi spyod do// yang dag par spong ba rnams la mi skyed de// rdzu 'phru

57a1('bum): bdag gis gzugs la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi gzugs so de 'am/ bdag gis dor ba la spyang bar bya'o na'am/ bdag gi ter b.le ke'am/ bdag gis 'du

60a6('bum): snying rje chen po la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi snying rje chen po'o zhe'am/ bdag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi sangs rgyas kyi ches pa 'dres pa
60a7('bum): bco brgyad de zhe 'am/ bdag gis rgyurd tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi rgyur tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'i zhe 'am/ bdag gis lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la spyad
60a8('bum): par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o zhe 'am/ bdag gis phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la spyad par bya'o zhe'am/ bdag gi phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o zhe'am/ bdag
60b1('bum): gis dgra bcom pa nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi dgra bcom pa nyid do zhe 'am/ bdag gis rang byang chub la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rang byang chub be zhe 'am/ bdag gis lam gyi
60b2('bum): rnam pa shes pa nyid la spyad par ba'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid de zhe 'am/ bdag gis rnam pa thams cad mkhor ba nyid la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi rnam pa thams
60b3('bum): cad 'khyer ba nyid de zhe 'ar/ bdag gis bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la spyad par bya'o zhe 'am/ bdag gi bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub be zhes bya bar bdag
60b4('bum): rang bdag gi bad pa med de/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub ni 'dzin pa la mi skyed/ mi 'dzin pa la mi spyod// rab 'byor gyis gsel ba/ bcom lngan
60b5('bum): 'das gal te de lngar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub 'dzin pa la'ang mi spyod da/ bya rkub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po'i byang chub ci la spyad pa
60b6('bum): lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de ji snyam du sems/ de bzhin gshegs pas sprul pa'i byang chub 'dzin pa 'am/ mi 'dzin pa 'am/ ci la
60b7('bum): yang skyed pa yeng dam/ gsel ba/ bcom ldan 'das de ri ma lags so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de ji snyam du sems/ dgra bcom pa'i rmi lam gyi blo
60b8('bum): 'dzin pa 'am/ mi 'dzin pa'ang skyed dam/ gsel ba/ bcom ldan 'das de ri pa lags te/ bcom ldan 'das dgra bcom pa la yeng yang nyal ba ma mchis ra/ de'i rmilamagyi che
61a1('bum): mi 'dzin pa la spyod par 'gyur ba lta ga la mchis/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' ser po'i byang chub kyang 'dzir
61a2('bum): ba 'am/ pi 'dzir pa la spyod pa med do// gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das gal te de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i byang chub 'dzir ba la'ang mi spyod/ mi 'dzin pa la'ang mi
61a3('bum): spyod/ gzugs la'ang mi spyod/ tshor ba la'ang mi spyod/ 'du shes la'ang mi spyod/ 'du byed la'ang mi spyod/ rnam par shes pa la yang pi spyod/ mig la'ang mi spyod/ rna ba la
61a4('bum): 'ang mi spyod/ sA la 'ang mi skyed/ lce la'ang mi spyod/ lus la'ang mi spyod/ yid la'ang mi spyod/ gzugs la 'ang mi spyod/ sgra la'ang mi spyod/ dri la'ang mi spyod
61a5('bum): rol yang mi spyod/ reg la'ang mi spyod/ chos rnams la 'ang mi spyod/ mig gi rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod rna ba'i rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ sna'i
61a6('bum): rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ lce'i rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ lus kyi rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ yid kyi rnam par shes pa la'ang mi spyod/ mig gi 'dus te reg
61a7('bum): ba la'ang mi spyod/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa la'ang mi spyod/ sna'i 'dus te reg pa la'ang mi skyed/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa la'ang mi spyod/ lus kyi 'dus te reg pa la'ang mi spyod/ yid
61a8('bum): kyi 'dus te reg pa la'ang mi spyod do// mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyer gyis tshor ba la'ang mi skyed/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la'ang mi spyod/ sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyer gyis
61b1('bum): tshor ba la'ang pi skyed/ lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyer gyis tshor ba la'ang mi spyod/ lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la'ang po skyed/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyer gyis dor ba la'ang mi
61b2('bum): spyod// sa'i khams la'ang mi skyed/ chu'i khams la'ang mi skyed/ me'i khams la'ang mi spyod/ rlung gi khams la'ang pi spyod/ na mkha'i khams la'ang mi spyod/ rnam par
61b3('bum): shes pa'i khams la'ang mi spyod/ ma rig pa la'ang ba spyod/ 'du byed la'ang mi sbed/ rnam par shes pa la'ang mi skyed/ ming dang gzugs la'ang mi spyod/ skye ma ched dgul
61b4('bum): 'ang ri spyod/ reg pa la'ang mi skyed/ dor ba la'ang mi skyed/ sred pa la'ang mi skyed/ len pa la 'ang pi skyed/ srid pa la'ang mi spyod/ skye ba la
61b5('bum): 'ang mi skyed/ rga shi la'ang mi spyod/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu pin pa la'ang mi skyed/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyir pa la'ang mi skyed/ bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyir pa la
61b6('bum): 'ang mi skyed/ brtser 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la'ang mi skyed/ bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa la'ang mi spyod/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la'ang mi skyed/ 
61b7('bum): rang stong pa nyid la'ang mi spyod/ phyi steng pa nyid la'ang mi spyod/ pi rang steng pa nyid la'ang mi spyod/ steng pa nyid stong pa nyid la'ang mi skyed/ chen po steng pa nyid
61b8('bum): la'ang mi skyed/ dor dam pa steng pa nyid la'ang mi skyed/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid la'ang mi skyed/ 'dus pa byas stong pa nyid la'ang mi skyed/ mtha' las 'das pa sbeng pa
62a1('bum): nyid la'ang mi spyod/ thog pa dang thar med pa stong pa nyid la'ang mi skyed/ dor ba med pa stong pa nyid la'ang mi skyed/ rang bzhin steng pa nyid la'ang mi spyod
62a2('bum): chos thams cad stong pa nyid la 'ang mi spyod/ rang gi mngon nyid stong pa nyid la'ang mi spyod/ mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid la'ang mi spyod/ dngos po med pa stong pa nyid la'ang mi skyed/ 
62a3('bum): de bo nyid steng pa nyid la'ang mi spyod/ dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid la'ang mi spyod// drar pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi la'ang mi sbed/ yang dag par spong ba bzhi la'ang mi sbed
62a4('bum): rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi la'ang mi skyed/ dbang po lnga la 'ang mi skyed/ stobs lnga la'ang mi skyed/ byang chub kyi yar lag bdud la'ang mi skyed/ 'phags
62a5('bum): pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa la'ang mi skyed/ 'phag sa pa'i bden pa bzhi la'ang mi spyod/ bsam gtan bzhi la'ang pi skyed/ tshad med pa bzhi la'ang mi
62a6('bum): skyeng / gzugs meng ba'i sems par 'jug pa bzhi la'ang mi spyad/ rnam par thar pa brgyad la'ang mi skyed/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i sems par 'jug pa dgu la'ang mi spyod/ 
62a7('bum): rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smod pa med pa la'ang mi spyod/ mngon par shes pa rnams la'ang mi spyod/ ting nge 'dzin rnams la'ang mi
62a8('bum): spyod/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams la'ang mi skyed/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la'ang mi skyed/ mi 'jigs pa bzhi la'ang mi spyod/ so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi
62b1('bum): la'ang mi skyed/ byams pa chen po la'ang mi skyed/ snying rje chen po la'ang mi spyod/ sangs rgyas kyi ches pa 'dres pa bco brgyad la'ang mi spyod// rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu la'ang mi spyod/ 
62b2('bum): lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la'ang mi skyed/ phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu la'ang mi spyod/ dgra bcom pa la'ang mi spyod/ rang byang dub la'ang mi spyod/ lam gyi rnam pa shes pa
62b3('bum): nyi la'ang mi spyod/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyed pa nyid la'ang yi spyod na// ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po pha rol tu phyir pa drug la spyod/ sdong pa nyid bcu bzhi dang / 
62b4('bum): byang chub kyi phyogs kyi nges sum cu rtsa bdud dang / rnam bar thar pa'i sgo gsum dang / bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzir dang / stobs
62b5('bum): par 'jug pa thams cad dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang / seM sa yang dag par rig pa bzhi dang / byams pa chen po dang / 
62b6('bum): snying rje re po dang / sangs rgyas kyi ches pa 'dres pa bco brgyad la smad/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa yongs su rdzogs par bgyis/ mngon par shes pa lnga la gnas/ byang chub
62b7('bum): sems dpa'i skyer ba ma ris pa la zhugs/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par bgyis/ sems cad yongs su smir bar bgyis/ mi cher po'i mngar sum cu rtsa gnyis
62b8('bum): dang dpe byang bzang po brgyad cu yongs su bsgrubs shing / rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das pha rol tu phyin
63a1('bum): badrug la la spyad/ stong pa nyid bcu bzhi lam spyang/ byang chub kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdud la pa smad/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum la la spyad/ bas pa gtar dang
63a2('bum): rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par 'jug pa thams cad la ma spyad/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la la spyad/ mi 'jigs pa bzhi la ma spyad/ so se yang
63a3('bum): dag par rig pa bzhi la pa spyad/ byams pa cher po la ma spyad/ snying rje re dpe la ba spyad/ sangs rgyas kyi ches pa 'dres pa bco brgyad la ma spyad/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu yongs su
63a4('bum): rdzogs par ma bgyis/ mngon par shes pa lnga la ma gnas byang chub sems dpa'i skyer pa ma chis par ma zhugs/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par la bgyis/ sems
63a5('bum): car rnams yongs su smir bar ma bgyis mi chen po'i marar sum cu rtsa gnyis dang / dpe byad bzang po brgyad cu yongs su pa bsgrubs par ri bla na med pa yang dag
63a6('bum): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar mi rus so// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byer de de bzhin ro// de de bzhin te/ de ji skad du smras
63a7('bum): pa bzhin te/ pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par ma byas steng ba nyid bcu bzhi dang / byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum cu rtsa bdun dang / rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum dang / 
63a8('bum): bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyems par 'jug pa thams cad dang / de bzhir gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa ba
63b1('bum): dang / so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi dang / byams pa chen po dang / snying rje chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos pa 'dres pa bco brgyad yengasu rdzogs par ma bas/ byang chub sems
63b2('bum): dpa'i sa bcu yongs su ma rdzogs/ mngon par shes pa lnga la pa gnas/ byang chub sems dpa'i skyer med par ma zhugs/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par ma byas/ sems cad
63b3('bum): rnams yongs su smin par la byas/ pi chen po'i mtshar sum cu rtsa gnyis dang / dpe bad bzang po brgyad cu yongs su ma bsgrubs par bla ra med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mar
63b4('bum): par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar mi rus te/ rab 'byor byang rkub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen nges pa rol tu phyin pa drug yongs su rdzogs par byas/ sbeng pa nyid
63b5('bum): thams cad dang / drad panye bar gzhag pa bzhi dang / yang dag par spong ba bzhi dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi dang / dbang po lnga dang / stobs lnga dang
63b6('bum): byang dub kyi yang lag bdud dang / 'phags pa'i lam yang lag brgyad pa dang / rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mdzar pa red pa dang / sper ba med pa dang / bsam gdar
63b7('bum): dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzir dang / snyoms par 'jug pa thams cad dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang / se se yang dag
63b8('bum): par rig pa bzhi dang / byams pa den po dang / snying rje rer po dang / sangs rgyas kyi nges pa 'dres pa bco brgyad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i skyer meng par zhugs/ sangs rgyas
64a1('bum): kyi nang yongs su dag par byas/ sems can rnams yongs su spor bar byas/ pi che po'i mngar sum cu rtsa gnyis dang / dpe byang bzang po brgyad cu yongs
64a2('bum): bsgrubs/ mi nyam pa'i chos nyid dang / rtag tu btang sems su spyod pa yongs su rdzogs par byas ras/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyer ba nyid theb par 'gyur ro// rab 'ber de yang
64a3('bum): gzugs kyi rang bzhir la gnas/ dor ba'i rang bzhir la gnas/ 'du shes kyi rang bzhin la gnas/ 'du byed kyi rang bzhir la gnas/ rnam par shes pa'i rang ba'ir la

64b8('bum): bzhin la gnas/ sbyid pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i rang bzhin la gnas/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i rang bzhin la gnas/ bzed pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i rang bzhi la
65a1('bum): gnas/ brtser 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyir pa'i rang bzhin la gnas/ bsam gdar gyi pha rol tu phyir pa'i rang bzhin la gnas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i

66b1('bum): 'am/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tsher ba 'am/ sa'i khams sam/ rku'i khams sa pa/ me'i khams sam/ rlung gi khams sam/ na mkha'i khams sar/ rnam par

66b5('bum): nang steng pa nyidi dang/ steng pa nyid stong pa nyid dang/ chen po stong pa nyid dam/ don dpa pa steng pa nyid dang/ 'dus byas stong pa nyid dam/ 'dus pa byas

66b7('bum): cang stong pa nyid dang/ rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid da/ mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid dam/ dngos po med pa stong pa nyid dang/ ngo bo nyid steng pa nyid dang/ dngos pa
66b8('bum): med pa'i ngo ba 'ang steng pa nyid ngadapa// drar panye bar gzhag pa rnams sam/ yang dag par spong ba rnams sapa/ rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa rnams sam/ dbang po rnams sa
67a1('bum): stobs rnams sam/ byang chub kyi yang lag rnams dang / 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa 'am// 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams sam/ bsapa gtar rnams

67a3('bum): par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyidri ma/ mtshan pa med pa dang / spen pa med pa 'am/ mngon par shes pa rnams sam/ ting nge 'dzin rnams sam/ gzungs kyi sgo rnams sam/ de bzhin

67b1('bum): dmigs so// rab 'byor de ji sam du sems/ gang gi tshe rab 'byor khyod kyis 'jig tshogs la lta ba spang ba'i phyir/ dbang po rnams thob par gyur pa dang / bar chad med pa'i ting nge 'dzir tam/

67b6('bum): rjer gyi tha snyad du bdags pa'o// tsher ba yang 'jig rten gyi tha snyad du bdags pa'o// 'du shes kyang 'jig rteran gyi tha snyad du btags pa'o// 'du byed kyang 'jig rter gyi tha snyad du bdags

79b4('bum): spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam par thar pa brgyad sgom yang rnam par thar pa rnams dang / rnam par thar pa sgom pa yang mi dmigs/ ches de gnyis las gzhan du'ang po skyed na
79b5('bum): de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rib kyi pha rol tu
79b6('bum): phyin pa la de ltar spyod na/ thabs mkhas pas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang ram byang
79b7('bum): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu sgom yang mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyems par
79b8('bum): 'jug pa rnams dang / mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa sgom pa yang mi dmigs/ chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyod na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems
80a1('bum): dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod ra/

80a3('bum): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan pa med pa dang / smon pa med pa sgom yang rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshar pa med pa dang / 
80a4('bum): smod pa med pa dang / rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshan pa med pa dang / smon pa med pa sgom pa yang mi dmigs/ chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyod ra/

80a6('bum): la de ltar spyod na/ thabs mkhas pas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang rang byang chub sems dpa' sems
80a7('bum): dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ mngon par shes pa rnams sgom yang mngon par shes pa rnams dang / mngon par shes pa sgom pa yang mi dmigs/ chos
80a8('bum): de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyod na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes
80b1('bum): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod na/ thabs ma bas pas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang ram byang chub
80b2('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ ting nge 'dzin rnams sgom yang ting nge 'dzin rnams dang / ting nge 'dzin sgom pa yang mi dmigs
80b3('bum): chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyod na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam theb par 'gyur te/ rab 'byer byang chub sems dpa' sems
80b4('bum): dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar skyed na/ thabs mkhas pas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzo gas pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// 
80b5('bum): rab 'byor gzhan yang ram byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tsha/ gzungs kyi ske rnams sgom yang gzungs kyi skye
80b6('bum): rnams dang / gzungs kyi sgo sgom pa yang mi dmigs/ chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mo spyod ra/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po byang chub kyi lam
80b7('bum): theb par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod ra/ thabs mkhas pas/ bla ra med pa yang dag
80b8('bum): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang rab byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i
81a1('bum): de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu skem yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs sgom pa yang mi dmigs/ chos
81a2('bum): gnyis las gzharan du'ang mi spyod na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' che dpe byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' med pa

81a4('bum): nar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i mi 'jigs pa bzhi sgem yang mi 'jigs pa rnams dang / mi 'jigs
81a5('bum): pa sgom pa yang mi dmigs/ chos de gnyis las gnan du'ang mi spyod / de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam theb par 'gyur te/ 
81a6('bum): rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod// thabs mkhas pas/ bla dmed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon
81a7('bum): par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang ram byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i re/ so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi
81a8('bum): skem yang so so yang dag par rig pa rnams dang / so so yang dag par rig pa skem pa yang mi dmigs/ chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi skyed na/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa'
81b1('bum): sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam theb par 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyir pa la de ltar spyod ra/ thabs mkhas pas/

81b3('bum): phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ snying rje cher po sgrim yang snying rje rer po dang / snying rje cher po skem pa yang mi dmigs chos de gnyis las gnar du'ang mi spyod ra/ de'i tshe byang chub
81b4('bum): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob par 'gyur te/ rab 'byer byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar spyod ra/ thabs
81b5('bum): mkhas pas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i bya nganub tu mngen par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// rab 'byor gzhan yang ram byang chub sems dpa' sems
81b6('bum): dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi ches ma 'dres pa bco brgyad sge ba yang sangs rgyas kyi chos pa 'dres pa rnams dang / sangs
81b7('bum): rgyas kyi chos pa 'dres pa sgom pa yang mi dmigs/ chos de gnyis las gzhan du'ang mi spyad da/ de'i ro byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub kyi lam thob par
81b8('bum): 'gyur te/ rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la de ltar skyed ra/ thabs mkhas pas/ bla med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
82a1('bum): byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// de nas tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bus bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsel te// bcom ldan 'das ji lta
82a2('bum): na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyir pa la spyod pa'i ro/ byang chub kyi la pa la brtson par bgyid pa lags// bcom lngan 'das kyis bka' stsal
82a3('bum): pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' cher po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyir pa la sbed pa'i te/ thabs mkhas pas/ gzugs la mi skyer mi 'byeng
82a4('bum): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i gzugs la ngo bo nyid med de// rer rab mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar
82a5('bum): gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i tshor ba la ngo bo nyid medang ngo // 'du shes mi sbyor mo 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ 
82a6('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i 'du shes la ngo bo nyid med do// 'du byed la mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i 'du byed la ngo bo 'a

82b1('bum): de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rna ba la ngo bo nying med de// sna mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i sAl

82b3('bum): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i lus la ngo bo nyid med do// yid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe / de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba

83a1('bum): pa mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhen/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i mig gi rnam par shes pa la de bo zhing meng ngo // rna ba'i rnam par

83a8('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa la ngo bo nyid mang ngo // sna'i 'dus te reg pa pi sbyar mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i sna'i 'dus

84a1('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba la ngo bo nyid med do// yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyedan gyis tsher ba mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ ngo bo'i phyir

84a7('bum): sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rnam par shes pa'i khams la ngo bo nyid meng ngo // ma rig pa mi skyer mi 'byed de/

85a7('bum): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ngo bo nyid med do// rang steng pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i nang stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid

85b5('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i 'dus byas stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am
85b6('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i 'dus ma byas stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dpe
85b7('bum): bar bya ba'i mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ 
85b8('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i thog ma dang tha ma med pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// dor ba med pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye
86a1('bum): bar bya ba'i do ba med pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// rang bzhin stong pa nyid yi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zher/ de ri 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ 
86a2('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i rang bzhin steng pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// chos thams cad steng pa nyid mi skyer mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i
86a3('bum): chos thams cad stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rang gi
86a4('bum): mtshan nyid stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// mi dmigs pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mo 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i ming dmig
86a5('bum): pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med // dngos po med pa stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'byeng de/ de ci'i phyir zher/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i dngos
86a6('bum): pe med pa stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid mi sbyor mi 'bed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i ngo bo nyid
86a7('bum): stong pa nyid la ngo bo nyid meng ngo // dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid pi spyir mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i dngos
86a8('bum): po med pa'i ngo bo nyid steng pa nyid la ngo bo nyid med do// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa rnams mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya
86b1('bum): ba'i dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi la ngo bo nyid med do// yang dag par spong ba bzhi mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ri 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i
86b2('bum): yang dag par spong ba bzhi la ngo bo nyid med do// rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi mi sbyor po 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rdzu 'phrul gyi
86b3('bum): rkang pa bzhi la ngo bo nyid med do// dbang po lnga pi sbyor mo 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i dbang po lnga la ngo bo nyid meng de// 
86b4('bum): stobs lnga pi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ri 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i stobs lnga la ngo bo nyid med de// byang chub kyi yang
86b5('bum): lag bdun pi sbyor mi 'byed de/ ngo ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i byang chub kyi yang lag bdun la ngo bo nyid med ngo // 
86b6('bum): 'phags pa'i lam yang lag brgyang ba paM ster mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i 'phags pa'i lam yang lag brgyad pa la ngo bo 'di
86b7('bum): meng ngo // 'phags pa'i bder pa ba'o mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi la ngo bo nyid med // 
86b8('bum): bsam gtar bzhi mi sbyar mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zher/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i bsam gtar bzhi la ngo bo nyid meng ngo // rang med pa bzhi pa
87a1('bum): ster mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i tshang med pa bzhi la ngo bo nyid meng nge// gzugs med pa'i sems
87a2('bum): par 'jug pa bzhi pa ster mo 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba'ang/ dbye bar bya ba'i gzugs med pa'i sems par 'jug pa ba'i la ngo bo nyid med de// rnam
87a3('bum): par thar pa brgyad pa sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe ra/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rnam par thar pa brgyad la ngo bo nyid med // mthar gyis gnas pa'i sems
87a4('bum): par 'jug pa dgu pi skyer mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhen/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i mthar gyis garas pa'i sems par 'jug pa dgu la
87a5('bum): nyid med do// rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang mtshan ma med pa dang / spen pa mang ba pi sbrer mi 'a byed de/ de ci'i phyir zher/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba
87a6('bum): 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i rnam par thar pa'i sgo steng pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smod pa med pa la ngo bo nyid med do// mngon par shes pa rnams pi skyer mi 'byedadu
87a7('bum): nga ci'i phyir zher/ de 'i 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i mngon par shes pa rnams la ngo ba nyid med de// ting nge 'dzir rnams pi skyer mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir
87a8('bum): na/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin rnams la ngo bo nyid med do// gzungs kyi sgo rnams mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar
87b1('bum): gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i gzungs kyi sgo rnams la ngo bo nyid med do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu pi sbyar mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe ra/ de ni 'di ltar gang sbyar
87b2('bum): ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs rnams la ngo bo nyid med do// mi 'jigs pa bzhi mi sbyor ba 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ri 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'a
87b3('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i mi 'jigs pa rnams leng bo nyid med do// se se yang dag par rig pa bzhi mi sbyor mi 'byed de/ de ci'i phyir zher/ de ri 'di ltar gang sbyar ba 'am/ 
87b4('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i seM sa yang dag par rig pa rnams la dzi rban da med de// snying rje cher po la sbyor mi 'byeng de/ de ci'i phyir zher/ de ri 'di ltar gang sbyang ba 'am/ 
87b5('bum): dbye bar bya ba'i snying rje dpe la ngo bo nyid meng ngo // sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad pi sbyar ro/ 'byed do// de ci'i phyir ra/ de ni 'di ltar ga
87b6('bum): sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar bya ba'i sangs rgyas kyi ches ma 'dres pa rnams la ngo bo nyid med do// gsel ba/ bcom lngan 'das chos gang la yang gang sbyar ba 'am/ dbye bar
87b7('bum): bgyi ba'i ngo bo nyid ma ma ri sa ra/ gang la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos bslab par bgyi ba'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ji ltar mngor bar 'grub par 'gyur/ 
87b8('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ma bslabs par ri/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos bla ra med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngor par rdzogs par 'a
88a1('bum): rgya bar ma nus pa// bcom ldan 'das shes bka' stsal pa/ shar 'i bung de bzhin na// rang bzhid / dzi skang du smras pa ban
88a2('bum): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la ma bslabs par byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos bla ra med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs
88a3('bum): par 'tshang rgya bar mi nus te/ de yang thabs mkhas pas yin gyi/ thabs mi mkhas pas pa yid de// sha ra dwa ti'i bu gal te byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
88a4('bum): chen po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ chos gang la la zhig gi ngo bo nyid dmigs na ni de'i phyir 'dzin par yang gyur na 'or te/ mi dmig
88a5('bum): na 'di ni gzugs so// 'di ni tshor ba'o// 'din 'du shes so// 'di ni 'du byed de// 'din rnam par shes pa'o zhes bya bar yang ci zhig gzung
88a6('bum): 'di dag ni skye mched rnams so// 'di dag ni khams rnams so// 'di ri rder cing 'brel par 'byung ba'o// 'di ri ma rig pa'o// 'di ni 'du byed de// 'di ni rnam par
88a7('bum): shes pa'o// 'di ni ming dang gzugs so// 'dini skye mched drug go// 'di ni rig pa'o// 'di ni tshor ba'o// 'di ni sred pa'o// 'di ni ler pa'o// 'di ni srid pa'o// 
88a8('bum): 'di ni skye ba'o// 'di ni rga shi'o// 'di ni sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni brtson
88b1('bum): 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ri bsapa gtar gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'di ri nang stong pa nyid de// 'di ni phyi steng pa nyid do// 'dir
88b2('bum): phyi nang steng pa nyid de// 'di ni stong pa nyid stong pa nyid de// 'odi ni chen po stong pa nyid do// 'di ni don dam pa steng pa nyid do// 'di ni 'dus byas stong pa nyid do// 'di ni 'dus
88b3('bum): ma byas steng pa nyid de// 'dir mtha' las 'das pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ri theg pa dang thar med pa steng pa nyid do// 'di ri dir ba med pa stong pa nyid do// 'di ni rang bzhin stong
88b4('bum): pa nyid // 'dir ches thams cad stong pa 'ad de/ 'di ni rang gi mtshan nyid stong pa nyid de// 'di ni mi dmigs pa stong pa nying ngo // 'dor dngos pa
88b5('bum): med pa steng pa nyid de// 'di ring bo nyid stong pa nyid do// 'di ni dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid stong pa nyid do// 'di dag ri dra pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi'o// 'di dag
88b6('bum): ni yang dag par spong ba bzhi'o// 'di dag ri rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi'o// 'di dag ri dbang po lnga'o// 'di dag ri stobs lnga'o// 'di dag ni byang chub kyi yan lag 'dud
88b7('bum): ni/ 'di dag ni 'phags pa'i lal yang lag brgyad pa'o// 'di dag ni 'phags pa'i bder pa bzhi'o// 'di dag ni bsam gtan bzhi'i// 'di dag ni tshang med pa
88b8('bum): bzhi'i'o// 'di dag ni gzugs med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhi'o// 'di dag ri rnam par thar pa brgyad do// 'di dag ri mthar gyis gnas pa'i skams par 'jug pa
89a1('bum): dgu'o// 'di dag ni rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mdzar pa med pa dang / sper pa med pa'o// 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i stengs

89a3('bum): brgyad de// 'di ni rgyun tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu'o// 'di ni lan cig phyir 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o// 'di ni phyir mi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu'o// 'di ni dgra bcom pa nyid de/ 
89a4('bum): 'di ni rang byang chub bo// 'di ni lam gyi rnam pa shes pa nyid do// 'di ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyer pa nyid de zhes bya bar yang ci zhig gzung ste/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu shes

89a7('bum): gzung du med pa'o// phyi steng pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// phyi nang stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// stong pa nyid stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// chen po stong pa nyid ni gzung
89a8('bum): du med pa'o// den dam pa steng pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// 'dus byas stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// 'dus pa byas stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// mtha' las 'das
89b1('bum): pa stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// thog ma dang tha ma med pa steng pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// dor ba med pa stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o// rang bzhin stong pa nyid ni gzung du med pa'o//

89b4('bum): yang dag par sbeng ba bzhi ri gzung du med pa'o// rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi ri gzung du med pa'o// dbang po lnga ra gzung du med pa'o// stobs lnga ri gzung du med pa'o//

89b6('bum): bsam gtar bzhi ni gzung du med pa'o// tshad med pa bzhi ni gzung du med pa'o// gzugs med pa'i snyems par 'jug pa bzhi ni gzung du med pa'o// rnam par thar pa brgyad
89b7('bum): ni gzung du med pa'o// mthar gyis gnas pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dgu ri gzung du med pa'o// rnam par thar pa'i sgo stong pa nyid dang / mtshar pa med pa dang / 
89b8('bum): smon pa med pa ri gzung du med pa'o// mngon par shes pa rnams ni gzung du med pa'o// ting nge 'dzir rnams ni gzung du med pa'o// gzungs kyi ske rnams ri gzung du mang
90a1('bum): pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu ni gzung du med pa'o// mi 'jigs pa bzhi ri gzung du med pa'o// skye so yang dag par rig pa bzhin

90a8('bum): pa ni gang zhig yeng/ rang sangs rgyas ni gang zhig yod/ byang chub sems dpa' ni gang zhig yeng/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
90b1('bum): rgyas ni gang zhig yeng / gal te gang zag de dag darigs su med na/ ches gang gis so so'i skye bo 'am/ rgyun tu zhugs pa 'am/ lan cig phyir 'ong ba 'am/ phyir mi 'ong ba

90b6('bum): kyi dngos po gang la byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams mngon par zhen par gyur pa de lta bu yed dam/ yed par gyur ta pa/ yod par 'gyur ram/ gsel ba/ bcom ldan

207a8('bum): ngan pa'i sems 'ga' tsam gyi go skabs kyang mi dbye'o// phyis 'gyod pa can du gyur ta re zhes chos ston to// sems can phan tshun gnod sems su gyur pa ji snyed pa de dag la la
207b1('bum): skad du ches sted te/ de ltar khyed gcig la gcig gnod sems su ma byed cig/ sems 'khrugs par gyur pa la dge ba'i ches gang yang skye bar mi 'gyur te/ de lta bas na khyed par

208a3('bum): bya bar mi nus ra/ gzhan gyi don lta ci smos te/ gang shes rab 'chal pa'i rnam par smin pa ni sems can dpral ba 'am/ byol seng gi skye gnas sam/ ga shir rje'i 'jig

208a5('bum): chags kyi spyod pa can gang ji snyed pa de dag mi sdug pa la sbyor// zhe sdang gi spyod pa can gang ji snyed pa de dag byams pa la sbyor ro// gti mug gi spyod pa car gang ji snyed pa de dag
208a6('bum): rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la sbyor ro// lam ngan par zhugs pa gang ji snyed pa de dag yang dag pa'i lam la sbyor te/ nyan thos kyi lam 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi lam 'am/ 
208a7('bum): sangs rgyas kyi lam la sbyor zhing de dag la 'di skad du chos steran to// khyed ches gang la mngon par zhen par gyur pa'i ches de dag ni ngo bo nyid kyis stong ste/ ngo bo nyid kyis stong

208b1('bum): chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ mngon par shes pa rnams la gnas shing / sems can rnams kyi dor byed pa yin no// de lha'i mig rnam par dag pa mi las

220b3('bum): du gyur ta re zhes tshes sten to// sems can phan tshun gnod sems su gyur pa ji snyed pa de dag la 'di skad du chos ster te/ de ltar khyed gcig la gcig gnong sems su
220b4('bum): ma byed cig/ sems 'khrug par gyur pa la dge ba'i ches gang yang skye bar mi 'gyur te/ de lta bas na khyed par tshun sems 'khrug par gyur ra/ sems can dpral
220b5('bum): bar skye ba 'am/ byol seng gi skye gnas su skye ba 'am/ gshin rje'i 'jig rten du skye ba'i gnas yod kyis/ de bas na khyed kyis 'khrug pa'i sems 'ga'
220b6('bum): tsam gyi ge skabs kyang mi dbye'o// phyis 'gyed pa can du gyur ta re zhes ches ston to// sems can le le can gang dza snyes de dag la 'di skad du chos sten te/ kye skyes bu dag
220b7('bum): le le ni sdug bsngal ba ste/ le les ni bdag gi nger kyang bya bar mi rus ra/ gzhan gyi den lta ci spes te/ le lo'i rnam par srid pa ni sems cad dmyal ba 'am/ byol seng ge
220b8('bum): skye gnas sam/ gshin rje'i 'jig rten yin te/ de ltar khyed ngar seng gsum du lhung ra/ bdag cag kyang gden par mi nus ra/ gzhan gded pa lta ci spos kyis
221a1('bum): de'i phyir khyed kyis le le'i sems 'ga' tsam gyi ge skabs kyang mi dbye'o// phyis 'gyed pa can du gyur ta re zhes ches ster to// sems car sems g.yeng ba
221a2('bum): gang ji snyed pa de dag la 'di skad du ches ster te/ kye skyes bu dag sems g.yeng ba ni sdug bsngal ba ste/ gang sems g.yeng ba'i rnam par smin pa ni sems can dpal ba 'am/ bye la seng gi skye
221a3('bum): ga ras sam/ gshin rje'i 'jig rten yin te/ de ltar khyed ngan seng gsum du lhung na/ bdag cag kyang gdod par mi nus na/ gzhan gden pa lta ci smos kyis/ de'i phyir khyed kyis
221a4('bum): g.yeng ba'i sems 'ga' tshal gyi ge skabs kyang mi dbye'o// phyis 'gyod pa cad du gyur ta re zhes ches ston to// sems can shes rab 'chal pa car gang ji snyed pa de dag la
221a5('bum): 'di skad du nges ston te/ kye skyes bu dag shes rab 'chal pa ni sdug bsngal ba ste/ shes rab 'chal pas ni bdag gi den kyang bya bar mi nus ra/ gzhar gyi dod lta ci skyes te/ 
221a6('bum): gang shes rab 'chal pa'i rnam par smin pa ni sems can dmyal ba 'am/ bye la seng gi skye gnas sam/ gshin rje'i 'jig rten yin te/ de ltar khyed kyis shes rab 'chal pa'i sems
221a7('bum): 'ga' tsam gyi ge skabs kyang mi dbye'o// phyis 'gyed pa can du gyur ta re zhes chos sten te// 'dod rags kyi spyod pa can gang ji snyed pa de dag ni mi sdug pa la sbyar ro// zhe sdang gi
221a8('bum): spyod pa can gang ji snyed pa de dag ri byams pa la sbyar re// gti mug gi spyod pa can gang ji snyed pa de dag ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba la sbyor ro// lam ngan par zhugs pa gang ji snyed pa de
221b1('bum): ngag yang dag pa'i lam la sbyar te/ nyan thos kyi lam 'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi lam 'am/ sangs rgyas kyi lam la sbyor zhing de dag la 'di skad du ches ster te/ khyed chos gang la mang/ 
221b2('bum): par zhen par gyur pa'i ches de dag ni ngo bo nyid kyis steng ste/ ngo bo nyid kyis steng pa'i ches rnams ri mngon par zhed par mi nus te/ stong pa nyid la mngon par zhed pa med de zhes chos ster
221b3('bum): te/ rab 'byor de ltar ra byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa'i tshe/ mngon par shes pa rnams la gnas shing / sems cad rnams
221b4('bum): kyi der byed pa yid ni// rab 'byor byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos ni mngon par shes pa rnams lam gnas par ni/ sems cad rnams la chos bstan par
221b5('bum): mi rus te/ la mgel bar zhugs pa'i sems can rnam sa kyang lam du gzung bar mi nus so// rab 'byor 'di ltar dper rabya mdab ma med pas ri/ ra mkha' la
221b6('bum): 'gro bar mi nus so// rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos kyang mngon par shes pa rnams la ma brten par sems can rnams la chos bstan bar mi nus// 
221b7('bum): rab 'byer de lta bas na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' ched pe shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la skyed pa'i tshe/ mngon par shes pa rnams mngod par sgrub par byas te/ de mngon par
221b8('bum): shes pa bangon par bsgrub pa de dag gis sems can rnams kyi ded ji bya bar dga' ba de bde bar byed de// des lha'i mig gis shar phyogs kyi 'jig rter gyi khams gang ga'i klung gi bye ma sed
222a1('bum): mthong ste/ de dag du sems cad gang ji snyed cig skyes pa de dag mthong ngo // de ltar mthong nas kyang rdzu 'phrul gyis de dag du seng zhing / sems cad
222a2('bum): ngag gi sems sems kyis khong du dud par byas nas/ de dang 'thur par smin pa'i gtam 'am/ tshul khrims kyi gtam 'am/ bzed pa'i gtapa 'am/ brtser 'grus kyi gad ba 'ang/ 
222a3('bum): bsam gtar gyi gdapa 'am/ shes rab kyi gtam 'am/ 'phags pa'i bden pa'i gtab 'am/ 'byung ba'i gdam gyi bar du ches ster te// des lha'i mig gis lde phyogs kyi
222a4('bum): 'jig rter gyi khams gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed mthong ste/ de dag du sems cad ji snyed cig skyes pa de dag kyang ba theng ngo // de ltar mtheng ras kyang rdzu 'phrul gyis de dag du seng
222a5('bum): zhing sems can de dag gi sems sems kyis khong du chu dpar byas nas/ de dang 'thun par sbyin pa'i gtab 'am/ tshul khrims kyi gtab 'am/ bzod pa'i
222a6('bum): gtam 'am/ brtson 'grus kyi gang pa 'am/ bsam gtan gyi gtab 'am/ shes rab kyi gtam 'am// 'phags pa'i bden pa'i gtam 'am/ 'byung ba'i gtam gyi bar du chos

223a1('bum): gis shar lde'i phyogs pa rnams kyi 'jig rteran gyi khams gang gi'i klung gi bye ba snyed mazeng ste/ de dag du sems cad gang ji srid cig skyes pa de dag kyang mthong ngo /

223b1('bum): du chung bar byas nas/ de dang 'thun par sbyir pa'i gad ma 'am/ tshul khrims kyi gtam 'am/ bzod pa'i gtam 'am/ brtson 'grus kyi gtam 'am/ bsam gtan gyi gtam 'am/

224a1('bum): ba'i khams kyis 'di lta ste/ lha dang mi gnyis ka'i sgra yang thes te/ de shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gang ga'i klung gi bye ba sed dag na/ sangs rgyas

271a6('bum): ba'o// 'di lar cig phyir 'ong ba'o// 'dir phyir mi 'ong ba'o// 'di dgra bcom pa'o// 'di ni rang sangs rgyas so// 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i// 'di ni de bzhin gshegs
271a7('bum): pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas so zhes bgyi ba'i rnam par rtog pa de dag mi dmigs ra/ des so so'i skye bo'i skye bo rnams dang / rgyud du zhugs pa rnams dang / lar
271a8('bum): cig phyir 'ong ba rnams dang / phyir mi 'ong ba rnams dang / dgra bcom pa rnams dang / rang sangs rgyas rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang / de bzhir gshegs
271b1('bum): pa dgra bcem pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams khyad par pa bachis par 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ rab 'byer nga de bzhin re// de de bzhin

272a1('bum): ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa'i den 'tshal ba ltar na// sangs rgyas dkor pa reg kyang gzhar la/ ches dkon ma chog kyang gzhan te/ dge 'dus theg kyang
272a2('bum): gzhan la/ nges panyam pa nyid kyang gzhan zhig pa lags kyi/ bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas dkor la reg gang lags pa dang / nges dkor pa reg gang lags pa dang / dge 'dud dkar pa reg
272a3('bum): gang lags pa de nyid nges mnyam pa nyid de/ chos de dag thams cad ri ldan pa yang ma lags/ mi ldan pa yang ba lags/ gzugs pa ma ris pa/ bstan du ma mchis ga/ theg pa pa mchis pa/ ma ngan nyid gcig

272b1('bum): ches rnams rnam par dged par ma mdzad/ sems can dpral ba yod par mjer dam/ byel song gi skye garas yed bar mngon dam/ gshing rje'i 'jig rten med par mngon ram/ mi

272b8('bum): nam reg mir gyi lha yeng bar mjer rab/ na mkha' mtha' yas skye mched kyi lha yeng bar mngon nam/ rnam shes mtha' yas skye ba rnyed kyi lnga yeng bar mjer rab/ cung zad pang pa'i skye ba dang
273a1('bum): kyi lnga yod par mngod nam/ 'du shes med 'du shes med mir skye mched kyi lnga yed par bangon nas// sbyid pa'i pha rol tu phyir pa yod par mdod rang// tshul khrims kyi pha rol du phyir pa

273b1('bum): lag rnams med par mdzin dpa/ 'phags pa'i lam yang lag brgyad pa med par mngon nam/ 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams med par mngon nam/ bsam gtan rnams med par mngar ma

277b2('bum): shes pa'i chos nyid kyang gzhan// mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i chos nyid kyang gzhan/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i chos nyid kyang gzhan/ snga'i 'dus te reg pa'i chos nyid kyang gzhan
277b3('bum): lce'i 'dus te reg pa'i ches nyid kyang gzhan/ lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i ches nyid kyang gzhan/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i chos nyid kyang gzhan// mig gi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis
277b4('bum): cher ba'i chos nyid kyang gzhan/ rna ba'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'i chos nyid kyang gzhan/ sna'i 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'i chos nyid kyang gzhan/ lce'i
277b5('bum): 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'i chos nyid kyang ga zhad/ lus kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis tshor ba'i ches nyid kyang gzhan/ yid kyi 'dus te reg pa'i rkyen gyis

278a1('bum): sred pa'i chos nyid kyang gzhad/ len pa'i ngas nyi kyang gzhan/ sring batshangs nyid kya gzhang/ sgruba'i ngas yang kyang gnang / rgashi ngas nyi dgadang/ 
278a2('bum): 'dod chags kyi ches nyid kyang gzhan/ zhe sdang gi ches nyid kyang gzhan/ gti mug gi nges nyid kyang gzhan/ lta ba'i rngam pa'i ches nyid kyang gzhan// sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i nges 'di

279a1('bum): kyang gzhang/ 'dus byas kyi khams kyi nges nyid kyang gzhang/ 'dus pa byas kyi khams kyi chos nyid kyang ga'an// bcom ldan 'das ji ltar la bar 'di la 'dra ba'i
279a2('bum): ches rnams kyi nges nyid pa tshar nyid gcig par 'gyur ba lags// ches rnams rnam par dged par ro ji ltar 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' che po ni shes rab kyi pha rol tu byed

279b1('bum): ldan 'das rnams la bsnyen bkur bgyid pa lags// de dag du'ang dge ba'i rtsa ba skyed pa lags/ dge ba'i rtsa ba des sems cad rnams yongasu srid par bgyid pa lags// sangs rgyas

327a4('bum): rigs kyi bu deng slan cang khyod kyi rim gre dang / zhab ring ba gyi ba'i slad du bdag gi lus khyod la dngul lo// des bdag gi lus phul nas byang chub sems dpa' sa pas dpa'
327a5('bum): chen po chos 'phags kyi mdun du thal me sbyar te 'dug ge/ de nas tshong dben gyi bu me de dang 'khor lnga brgya de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' be pe rtag tu ngul 'a
327a6('bum): skad ces smras so// rigs kyi bu bdag cag kyang khyed la lus 'bul gyis/ bdag cag kyang dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis ches de dag thob par gyur cig/ khyed nyid dang lhan cig tu sangs rgyas rnams
327a7('bum): dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams la bkur sti bgyis pa dang / de dag dang nye bar gyur par bgyi'o// de ras byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu ngus tshong dper gyi bu me la
327a8('bum): sogs pa/ bu mo lnga brgya la 'di skad ces smras so// bu mo dag khyed cag khe be la lhag pa'i bsam pas gnas par byed na/ kho bo la lhag pa'i bsam pas bdag nyid byin cig dang / 
327b1('bum): bu me khyed khe bes blang ngo // bu me de dag gis smras pa/ khyed la lhag pa'i bsam pa thag pa nas khyed kyi rjes su mthun par 'jug go// khyed la lhag pa'i bsam pa ci 'dod pa bya bar bdag nyid
327b2('bum): 'bul lo// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu dus tshong dpon gyi bu mo la sogs pa bu me lnga brgya de dag rgyan thams cad kyis brgyan te/ shing rta lnga brgya yang brgyad ras/ 
327b3('bum): thams cad byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos 'phags la phul te/ rigs kyi bu bdag ni 'khor 'di dag dang / shing rta lnga brgya 'di dag kyang yongs su longs spyod pa'i phyir
327b4('bum): khyed la dbul le// de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis rigs kyi bu de la leg so zhes bya ba byin te/ rigs kyi bu legs so legaso// de ltar byang chub sems dpa'
327b5('bum): sems dpa' chen po dag gis bdog pa thams cad yongs su btang bar bya'o// yongs su gtong ba'i sems de lta bus myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang
327b6('bum): chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// de ltar na chos smra ba dag la mchod pa byas nas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang thabs la mkhas pa nyan nus te/ sngoran gyi de bzhin gshegs
327b7('bum): pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag gis kyang sngon byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa ra/ 'di lta bu'i gtong ba la gnas nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
327b8('bum): byang chub yang dag par bsgrubs te/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang thabs la mkhas pa yongs su dris so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos 'phags kyis tshong
328a1('bum): dpon gyi bu mo la sogs pa bumo lnga brgya pa de dag dang / shing rnga lnga brgyad de dag byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu ngu'i dge ba'i rtsa ba yongasu bskang bar
328a2('bum): phyir blangs te/ blangs nas rigs kyi bu rtag tu ngu de nyid la byin no// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos 'phags stan las langs te bdag kyi khyim du zhugs pa dang nyim
328a3('bum): nub par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu ngu 'di snyam du sems te/ 'di ltar bdag chos 'dod pa'i phyir 'ongs la/ 'dug pa 'am nyal ba byed pa ni
328a4('bum): bdag gi mi cha la/ 'di ni ma legs kyis byang chub sem sa dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos 'phags 'di lta ste/ chos ston tu phyir ma byung gi bar du/ bdag 'greng ba dang

328a6('bum): par zhugs par gyur cing / byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin grangs med dpag tu med pa dag dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang thabs la mkhas pa las byung ba la gnas
328a7('bum): par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu ngu yang lo bdun gyi bar du 'dod pa'i rtog pa ma byung / gnod sems kyi rtog pa ma byung / rnam par 'tshe ba'i rtog pa

328b1('bum): po chos 'phags chos kyi khri gang la rigs kyi bu de 'dug nas ches snyed par 'gyur ba'i ches kyi khri ba sha pa na/ bdag gis phyogs 'di chag chag legs par gdab pa dang / legs par byugs la ma
328b2('bum): teg sna tshogs gtor te/ sa phyogs gang du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos 'phags shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang thabs mkhas pa rab tu sten par 'gyur ba der legs par drug

328b5('bum): bdud na/ ting nge 'dzin 'di las ldang ste langs nas grong khyer gyi dbus su 'dug ste chos sted par 'gyur ro zhes grag ge/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag thung
328b6('bum): lnga'i sgra de thos pa dang / dga' ba dang / mgu ba dang / yid rangs pa dang / rab tu mgu zhing dga' ba dang / yid bde ba skyes te/ tshong dper gyi bu me la sogs pa bu me lnga brgya da
328b7('bum): sa phyogs de phyags nas chos kyi khri rin po che thams cad kyis spras pa bshams// de nas bu po de dag gis rang rang gi bla gos pud de sngar gang la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po

329a1('bum): gis chu bams cad mi snang bar byas nas ci nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu du chum rnyed nas yid mi dga' zhing sems sdug bsngal te/ sems
329a2('bum): gzhan du 'gyur ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba nub par 'gyur ba dang / mchod pa de yang mi mdzes par bya ba'i phyir tu de dag mi snang bar byas nas kun tu rku btsal na chu ma rnying ngo // de nas byang chub sems
329a3('bum): dpa' sams dpa' chen po rtag tu ngu 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gi lus phug la khrag gis sa phyogs 'di rtag chag gdab par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sa phyogs 'di ni rdul cha ste/

329a7('bum): gis sa phyogs de kho ra khor yug tu chag chag btab bo// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu ngu'i rjes su slob pa/ tshong dpon gyi bu mo la sogs pa bu mo lnga brgya de dag
329a8('bum): thams cad kyis kyang mtshon rnon po blangs te/ rang rang gi lus phug nas rang rang gi khrag gis sa phyogs de chag chag btab ste/ gang de dag la bdud sdig te can gyis dge ba'i phyogs kyi bar
329b1('bum): chad bya ba'i glags rnyed par mi 'gyur bar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu ngu dang / bu me de dag sems gzhan du gyur pa med do// de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin 'di snyam du

329b7('bum): mi khyab bo// khyed kyi chos 'dod pa dang / chos yongs su tshol ba bla na med do// rigs kyi bu sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag gis kyang
329b8('bum): lhag pa'i bsam pa 'di lta bu dang / brtser 'grus 'di lta bu dang / ches 'dod pa 'di lta bus bla ra med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub yang dag par bsgrubs so// de nas byang chub sems
330a1('bum): dpa' sems dpa' chen po rtag tu ngu 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ches 'phags kyi chos kyi skad ni bting / sa pags

330a7('bum): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ches 'phags lo bdun 'das pa dang / ting nge 'dzin de las langs te/ chos kyi stan gang na yod pa der 'ongs nas bstan bting ba la 'dug ste/ 'a

330b1('bum): dpa' sems dpa' chen po ches 'phags mthong ma thag tu/ 'di lta ste dper na/ bsam gtan dang po la spobs par zhugs pa'i dge slong rtse gcig tu yid la byed pa bzhin du bde ba de lta bu thob bo//

330b8('bum): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa sna tshogs pa nyid do// namakha' rtog pa med pa nyid pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rtag pa med pa nyid do// gzugs su med pa nyid pas shes rab kyi pha rol du
331a1('bum): phyir pa mu med pa nyid de// de bzhin du tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed rnams dang / rnam par shes pa bu med pa nyid pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa du med

331a8('bum): ches thams cad dben pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / ches thams cad g.yo ba med pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang / ches thams cad rlom sems med pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin dang
